## ğŸ¨ What is GPTâ€‘4o

GPTâ€‘4o is a multimodal model that not only turns text prompts into highâ€‘quality images but also offers imageâ€‘toâ€‘image editingâ€”enabling targeted retouching, style transfer, and multiâ€‘image blending.

- ğŸ§  Multimodal comprehension: Simultaneously parses text and images to capture creative intent with precision
- âœï¸ Accurate rendering: Handles complex prompts and rapidly produces highâ€‘quality images
- ğŸ¨ Diverse styles: Ghibli, painterly, pixel art, 3D plush, and moreâ€”pick your favorite
- ğŸ–¼ï¸ Realistic composition: Spatial depth, perspective, and lighting that feel authentic
- âœï¸ Easy postâ€‘editing: Swap backgrounds, tweak detailsâ€”seamless for secondâ€‘round creation
- âš¡ï¸ Lightningâ€‘fast interaction: Shorter response times for realâ€‘time ideation and iteration

<a id="tools-intro"></a>
## ğŸ› ï¸ Tools Introduction

Here are applications where you can use the GPT-4o model to generate images:

- **ğŸ’¬ [ChatGPT](https://chatgpt.com):** Official OpenAI product. Use GPT-4o to generate high-quality images with support for multiple styles and detailed control, suitable for creative expression and content creation.

- **ğŸ¬ [Sora](https://sora.com):** Official OpenAI product. Generate realistic images via GPT-4o, supporting text-image combination and scene reconstruction, suitable for visual creative scenarios like film and animation. *(Note: Sora access is currently limited)*
- **ğŸ¤– [gpt-image-1 API](https://platform.openai.com/docs/guides/image-generation)ï¼š** Officially developed by OpenAI, the latest image generation model can be accessed via API and provides:
  - âœ… More accurate, high fidelity images
  - ğŸ¨ Diverse visual styles
  - âœï¸ Precise image editing
  - ğŸŒ Rich world knowledge
  - ğŸ”¤ Consistent text rendering
